08/01/25, 1:47‚ÄØpm - +91 96258 96327: Please find attached the terms and conditions:
1. Breach of Bond
The condition that occurs if the Employee voluntarily resigns or is terminated for cause during the
Bond Period, obligating the Employee to repay the Company an amount equivalent to six (6)
months of their gross salary.
2. Gross Salary
The total salary earned by the Employee before any deductions, including but not limited to taxes
and social security contributions.
3. Annual Appraisal
The yearly evaluation of the Employee's performance, which may result in a salary increment
ranging from twenty percent (20%) to fifty percent (50%) based on the Employee‚Äôs performance.
4. Bonus
A financial reward paid to the Employee, ranging from eight point thirty-three percent (8.33%) up
to twenty-five percent (25%) of their annual salary, contingent upon the Company‚Äôs performance
and the Employee‚Äôs individual performance.
